<script>
var cookie_en = navigator.cookieEnabled;
if(cookie_en == 0)alert("You need to enable cookies for this site to load properly!");
cookie_name="stocks";
cookie_value="Maruti.Suzuki_MU01";
var expDays = 30;
var exp = new Date(); 
exp.setTime(exp.getTime() + (expDays*24*60*60*1000));
var val1="";
if(cookie_value.length>3)addcookievalue(cookie_name,cookie_value);
function getcookie(name)
{
	var m_cookies = (document.cookie).split(";");
	for(m_ctr=0; m_ctr < m_cookies.length; m_ctr++)
	{
		m_str = (m_cookies[m_ctr]).split("=");
		if(m_str[0] == " "+name || m_str[0] == name)
			return unescape(m_str[1]);
	}
	return "";
}
function addcookievalue(name, value)
{
	var other_value = "";
	var new_value = "";
	var val1="";
	old_value = getcookie(name);
	if((old_value).match(unescape(value)) == null)
	{
		mstr = old_value.split("|");
		for(var k=1;k<mstr.length;k++)
		{
			if(k<11)val1 = val1+"|"+mstr[k];			
		}
		val1=val1.replace('||','|');
		document.cookie = name + "=|" + escape(value) + "~1" + escape(val1) + "; expires=" + exp.toGMTString() + "; path=/; domain=.moneycontrol.com; ";
	}
	else
	{
		mstr = old_value.split("|");
		for(var k=1;k<mstr.length;k++)
		{
			if(k<11){
				val1 = val1+"|"+mstr[k];			
			}
		}
		val1=val1.replace('||','|');
		m_str = val1.substring(old_value.indexOf(value));
		m_val = m_str.split("~");
		m_newstr = eval(parseInt(m_val[1])+1);
		m_str = m_val[0] + "~" + eval(parseInt(m_val[1]));
		val1=val1.replace(m_str,'');
		val1=val1.replace('||','|');
		document.cookie = name + "=|" + escape(value) + "~"+escape(m_newstr) +'' + escape(val1) + "; expires=" + exp.toGMTString() + "; path=/; domain=.moneycontrol.com; ";
	}
}
function deletecookie(name)
{
	m_value = getcookie(name);
	document.cookie = name + "=" + m_value + "; expires=-1";
}
</script>

	    var i, x, y, cl = document.cookie.split(";");

	    if (x == "nnmc") { 
	    out.nnmc = unescape(y); 
	    c = c + 1

	    out._w18g = unescape(y);

	    out._w18s = unescape(y); 
	    c = c + 1 
	    }

	    return out 
	    } 
	    }

	    }

function _w18sub() {
	var _w18userinfo_out = {};
	if( typeof localStorage !== "undefined" ) {
		if( localStorage.getItem( "_w18userinfo" ) !== null ) {
			_w18userinfo_out = localStorage.getItem( "_w18userinfo" );
			_w18userinfo_out = unescape( _w18userinfo_out );
			var contact = JSON.parse( _w18userinfo_out );
			console.log('_w18userinfo_out = ', contact);
			for(var contactItem in contact){
			    //console.log("Key="+contactItem);
			    //console.log(contact[contactItem]);
			    if(contactItem == 'interest_channel' || contactItem == 'interest_bucket' || contactItem == 'logged_in' || contactItem == 'extra'){
				//console.log(contact[contactItem]);
				for(var contactItemVal in contact[contactItem]){
				    //console.log(contact[contactItem][contactItemVal]+"<<<<<<<<<<<>>>>>>>>>>>"+contactItemVal);
				    googletag.pubads().setTargeting( contactItemVal,contact[contactItem][contactItemVal] );
				}
			    }
			    else if(contactItem == 'vernacular' )
			    {
				//console.log(contact[contactItem]);
				googletag.pubads().setTargeting( contactItem,contact[contactItem] );
			    }
			    else if(contactItem == 'interest_platform' )
			    {
				//console.log("interest_platform");
				//console.log(contact[contactItem]);
				for(var contactItemVal in contact[contactItem])
				{
				    //console.log("interest_platform");
				    console.log(contactItemVal);
				    console.log(contact[contactItem][contactItemVal]);
				    googletag.pubads().setTargeting( contactItemVal,contact[contactItem][contactItemVal]);
				    for(var platform_name in contact[contactItem][contactItemVal] )
				    {
					//console.log(contact[contactItem][contactItemVal][platform_name]);
					//googletag.pubads().setTargeting( contactItemVal,contact[contactItem][contactItemVal][platform_name] );
				    }
				}
			    }
			};
		}
	}
	return false;
}

<script type="text/javascript">
function _w18setuserbehaviour(){ //_w18userinfo
	var i, x, y, cl = document.cookie.split(";");
	var _w18userinfo_out = {};
	var _w18userdetail_out = {}; _w18userdetail_out._w18userdetail='';
	var c = 0;
	for (i = 0; i < cl.length; i++) {
		x = cl[i].substr(0, cl[i].indexOf("="));
		y = cl[i].substr(cl[i].indexOf("=") + 1);
		x = x.replace(/^\s+|\s+$/g, "");
		
		if (x == "_w18userinfo") {
			_w18userinfo_out._w18userinfo = unescape(y);
			c = c + 1
		}
		
		if (x == "_w18userdetail") {
					_w18userdetail_out._w18userdetail = unescape(y);
					c = c + 1
		}
		if (c == 2) {break;}
	}

	if(c==1 || c==2){
		var contact = JSON.parse(_w18userinfo_out._w18userinfo);
		
		for (var item in contact) {
			googletag.pubads().setTargeting(item,contact[item]);
			//console.log('item >> ',item,' ,contact >> ',contact[item]);
		}
		//console.log('before if lapsed_item');
		if(_w18userdetail_out._w18userdetail != '' || _w18userdetail_out._w18userdetail.length >0 ){
			//console.log('inside if lapsed_item');
			var lapsed_contact = JSON.parse(_w18userdetail_out._w18userdetail);
			if(_w18userdetail_out._w18userdetail){
				for (var lapsed_item in lapsed_contact) {
					googletag.pubads().setTargeting(lapsed_item,lapsed_contact[lapsed_item]);
					//console.log('lapsed_item >> ',lapsed_item,' ,lapsed_contact >> ',lapsed_contact[lapsed_item]);
				}
			}
		}
	}
} 

function _w18_lc_settargeting() {
	if(typeof localStorage !== "undefined") {
		//start of code
		if(localStorage.getItem("di_consume_articles") !== null) {
			var di_consume_articles_json = localStorage.getItem("di_consume_articles");
			if(!di_consume_articles_json || di_consume_articles_json !== null){
				var di_consume_articles_old_arr = JSON.parse(di_consume_articles_json);
				var default_list_json	=  '{"2089141":1, "1624181":1, "1623461":1, "1399696":1}';
				var default_list	=  JSON.parse(default_list_json);
			    //default_list = default_list.filter(function(n){ return n != undefined }); 
				var not_consume = new Array();//send to dfp
				for(key in default_list){
					if(di_consume_articles_old_arr[key] != 1){
						not_consume.push(key);
					}
				}
				if(not_consume.length>0){
					//console.log('not_consume >> ',not_consume);
					googletag.pubads().setTargeting('di_consume_articles',not_consume);
				}
			}else{
				//console.log('di_consume_articles not set in localStorage');
			}
		}
		//end of code
	}else {
		//console.log('localStorage not supported');
	}
}

//mctop_getCookie //dfpGutter_getCookie
//mctop_setCookie //dfpGutter_setCookie 

var dfp_date = new Date();
//var mc_mcmarketstockprice_gutter_ck = "MC_GUTTER_mcmarketstockprice_"+dfp_date.getFullYear()+"-"+(dfp_date.getMonth()+1)+"-"+dfp_date.getDate();

var mc_mcmarketstockprice_gutter_ck = "MC_GUTTER_mcmarketstockprice";


function close_mc_gutter(){
	dfpGutter_setCookie(mc_mcmarketstockprice_gutter_ck,1,1);		
}


function dfpGutter_setCookie(e,t,n){
	var r=new Date;
	r.setDate(r.getDate()+n);
	var i=escape(t)+(n==null?"":"; expires="+r.toUTCString())+"; path=/; domain=.moneycontrol.com; ";
	document.cookie=e+"="+i
}
function dfpGutter_getCookie(e){
	var t,n,r,i=document.cookie.split(";");
	for(t=0;t<i.length;t++){
		n=i[t].substr(0,i[t].indexOf("="));
		r=i[t].substr(i[t].indexOf("=")+1);
		n=n.replace(/^\s+|\s+$/g,"");
		if(n==e){
			return unescape(r)
			}
		}
}

			$('div.myaccpop').remove();
		}

		usernnmc = usernnmc.replace(/\+/g, " ");
		var dispnm = usernnmc;

		if( usernnmc.length > 6 ) {
			dispnm = usernnmc.substr( 0, 6 ) + '..';
		} else {
			dispnm = usernnmc;
		}

		$('strong#usr_nm, a#mobile_usr_nm').text("Hi "+dispnm);

	var timer;    
	$('.ads120x24').hide();

	$('#ads_wrapper').css({width:965,height:24});
	timer = setTimeout(function() { $(".ads965x24").fadeOut().removeClass('bannerLarge'); $('.ads120x24').fadeIn().addClass("banner_small"); $('.ads_wrapper').animate({width:120},0); }, 6000);
	
	$('#close').on('click',function(){

		 $('.ads120x24').addClass("banner_small").fadeIn();

});

<script type="application/javascript">
function findMyId() { //to get iframe id.
  // here u are getting the array of all the Ifremaes from the parent document.
  var iframes = top.document.getElementsByTagName("iframe");
  for (var i=0, len=iframes.length; i < len; ++i) {
	if (document == iframes[i].contentWindow || self == iframes[i].contentWindow) 
	{
	return iframes[i].id;
	}
  }
  return "";
}
function resizeIframe(){
		var iFrameId = findMyId(); //getting iframe id.
        var size=document.getElementById("ads_wrapper").offsetWidth;
		var parentElem = parent.document.getElementById(iFrameId);
		parentElem = parentElem.parentNode;
        if(parent.document.getElementById(iFrameId)){			
        	//parent.document.getElementById(iFrameId).style.height=size+"px";
			parentElem.setAttribute("style", "width:120px;height:24px;position: relative;display:block;overflow:visible;float:right;");
			parent.document.getElementById(iFrameId).setAttribute('style', 'width:'+size+'px; height:24px; border: 0px; padding: 0px; margin: 0px; top: 0px;clip: rect(0px 965px 24px 0px);z-index: 10000;right:0;position: absolute;');
        }
}
if (top != self) {setInterval(function(){resizeIframe()}, 100); }

});

<script type="text/javascript">
	// analytics functions start
	var KEY = "A18ID", DAYS = "730";
	
	function _htCreate(name,value,days) {
		var expires = "";
		if (days) {
			var date = new Date();
			date.setTime(date.getTime() + (days*24*60*60*1000));
			expires = "; expires=" + date.toUTCString();
		}
		document.cookie = name + "=" + value + expires + "; path=/";
	}
	
	function _htGet(name) {
		var nameEQ = name + "=";
		var ca = document.cookie.split(";");
		for(var i=0;i < ca.length;i++) {
			var c = ca[i];
			while (c.charAt(0)==" ") c = c.substring(1,c.length);
			if (c.indexOf(nameEQ) == 0) return c.substring(nameEQ.length,c.length);
		}
		return null;
	}
	
	function _htDel(name) {
		_htCreate(name,"",-1);
	}
	
	function getId() {
		return Date.now() + "." + Math.round(Math.random() * 1000000);
	}
	function create_dim_cookie(){
		ID = _htGet(KEY);
		if(null == ID || "" == ID) {
			ID = getId();
			_htCreate(KEY, ID, DAYS);
		}
	}
	// end analytics functions

	function getCookie(cname) {
		var name = cname + "=";
		var ca = document.cookie.split(';');
		
		for(var i = 0; i < ca.length; i++) {
			var c = ca[i];
			while (c.charAt(0) == ' ') {
				c = c.substring(1);
			}
			
			if (c.indexOf(name) == 0) {
				return c.substring(name.length, c.length);
			}
		}
		
		return "";
	}
	
	create_dim_cookie();

  })(window,document,'script','//www.google-analytics.com/analytics.js','ga');

					<script>

							function stkpatti_chkfeed(stock_name)

							{

								var prtmsgobj=document.port_msg_stk_patti.f_message;

								var tmp=prtmsgobj.value;

								var tgt_txt="";

								tmp.replace(" ","");

							 

								if(tmp=="" || tmp==$("#f_message_text").val())

								{

									alert("Please input your Message");

									prtmsgobj.value='';

									prtmsgobj.focus();

									return false;

								}

								

								if(!(readCookie('nnmc'))){
									AFTERLOGINCALLBACK = '$("#port_msg_stk_patti").submit();';
									$("#myframe").attr('src','https://accounts.moneycontrol.com/mclogin/?d=2&redirect=afterlogin');
									$("#LoginModal").modal();
									return false;
								}

								else{

									//return false;

									$("#port_msg_stk_patti").submit();

									$("#f_message").val('');

									closePop_mmb('aboutPage_mmb');

									closePop_mmb('TopCallout_stk');

								}

							}



							function verify_signin_exprhs(action)

							{

								if(action==2){

									$('#loginchk2').load($.post('/msgboard/guest_login_ajaxverify.php', '', function(data) 

									{		

										if(data=='alldone')

										{

											$("#port_msg_stk_patti").submit();

											closePop_mmb('aboutPage_mmb');

											closePop_mmb('TopCallout_stk');

										}

									}));

								}else{

									var f_id_pro = $("#f_id_pro").val();

									var f_pwd_pro = $("#f_pwd_pro").val();

									var rememberme_pro = $("#rememberme_pro").val();

									var keepsignin_pro = $("#keepsignin_pro").val();



									if(f_id_pro=="")

									{

									alert("Please enter your username");

									$("#f_id_pro").focus();

									return false;

									}

									else if(f_pwd_pro=="")

									{

									alert("Please enter your Password");

									$("#f_pwd_pro").focus();

									return false;

									}

									else if(f_id_pro!='' && f_pwd_pro!='')

									{

										$.get("/watchlist1/login_check.php",{sectionid:"M3",username:f_id_pro,password:f_pwd_pro,saveid:rememberme_pro,keep_signed:keepsignin_pro},function(data){



										if(data=="pwd")

										{

											$("#f_id_pro").val('');

											$("#f_pwd_pro").val('');

											$("#rememberme_pro").val('');

											$("#keepsignin_pro").val('');

											alert("Invalid Login.");

											return false;

										}

										else if(data=="alldone")

										{

											$("#port_msg_stk_patti").submit();

											closePop_mmb('aboutPage_mmb');

											closePop_mmb('TopCallout_stk');

										}

										});

									}

									return false;

								}

							}



							function popBox_mmb(div){	

								var popMargTop = ($('#'+div).height()) / 2;

								var popMargLeft = ($('#'+div).width()) / 2;

								$('#'+div).css({ 'margin-top' : -popMargTop, 'margin-left' : -popMargLeft });

								$("#"+div+"").show();

								//$('#lightbox_cb').remove();

								$('body').append('<div id="lightbox_cb"></div>'); 

								$('#lightbox_cb').css({'filter' : 'alpha(opacity=80)'}).show(); 

							}

							function closePop_mmb(div){ 

								$("#lightbox_cb, #"+div+"").hide();

							}



							function set_count(sc_name,scid,action){

								

								if(scid!="" && action!=""){

									if((readCookie(scid+'mc_stk_cnt'))!=1){

										$.ajax({

											"url":"/stocks/company_info/set_stock_count_ajax.php",

											"type":"post",

											"data":{"action":action,"scid":scid},

											success:function(result){

												//alert('ha ha ha');

											}

										});

									}else{

										$("#sent_thank").html("You are already voted!");

									}



									$('.pl_thankbx').show();

									if(action=='b')

										sent_act = 'buy';

									if(action=='s')

										sent_act = 'sell';

									if(action=='h')

										sent_act = 'hold';

									

									var sent_inner_txt = "Why do you think "+sc_name+" is a "+sent_act+"?";

									$("#f_message").val(sent_inner_txt);

									$("#f_message_text").val(sent_inner_txt);

<script type="text/javascript">
var $ = jQuery;
function get_company_result(sc_id,sc_fullname,sc_fullname1,step,ec_flag){
jQuery.ajax({
		type:"post",
		url:"/stocks/company_info/ajax_company_result.php",
		data:{sc_fullname:sc_fullname,sc_fullname1:sc_fullname1,sc_id:sc_id,ec_flag:ec_flag},
		success:function(data){
			if(data!=''){
				data = trim(data); 
				//alert(data);
				if(data!="NO DATA"){
				jQuery("#disp_result").html("");
				jQuery("#disp_result").html(data);
				jQuery("#disp_result").show();
				commonPopRHS('rslt_askmgmtPop');
				}
					
			}
		}
	});	
}

 function validate_ysu(param)
 {
	 var ask_mgmt = jQuery("#f_message_ask").val();
	 if(ask_mgmt==''){
		 alert('Please input your query here.'); 
		 jQuery("#f_message_ask").focus();
		 return false;
	 }
	 else if(ask_mgmt=='Go ahead and post your question'){
		 alert('Please input your query here.'); 
		jQuery("#f_message_ask").focus();
		 return false;
	 }
	 else if(ask_mgmt.length<5){
		 alert('Please input atleast 20 character.'); 
		 jQuery("#f_message_ask").focus();
		 return false;
	 }
	 else{
		if(param==0)
		{  
			jQuery('#lightbox_cb,#rslt_askmgmtPop').hide();
			work_div=3;		 
			check_login_pop(3);
		}
		else
		{
			document.form_ask_mgmt.f_message.value =jQuery("#f_message_ask").val();
			//jQuery("#f_message").val(ask_mgmt);
			jQuery("#form_ask_mgmt").submit();
			//jQuery("#f_message_ask").val('');
			//jQuery("#f_message_ask").val('Go ahead and post your question');
			return true;
		} 
	 }
 }
</script>

<script type="text/javascript" language="javascript">
function show_mktdata(tab_no)
{
	if(tab_no == "1")
	{
		document.getElementById("mktdet_head").innerHTML = "Standalone";
		$("#mktdet_nav_1").addClass('act');
		$("#mktdet_nav_2").removeClass('act');

		document.getElementById("mktdet_1").style.display = "block";
		document.getElementById("mktdet_2").style.display = "none";
	}
	else
	{
		document.getElementById("mktdet_head").innerHTML = "Consolidated";
		$("#mktdet_nav_1").removeClass('act');
		$("#mktdet_nav_2").addClass('act');		

		document.getElementById("mktdet_1").style.display = "none";
		document.getElementById("mktdet_2").style.display = "block";		
	}
}

function show_findata(tab_no)
{
	if(tab_no == "1")
	{
		//document.getElementById("findet_head").innerHTML = "Standalone";
		$("#findet_nav_1").addClass('act');
		$("#findet_nav_2").removeClass('act');

		document.getElementById("findet_1").style.display = "block";
		document.getElementById("findet_2").style.display = "none";

		document.getElementById("findet_11").style.display = "block";
		document.getElementById("findet_22").style.display = "none";
	}
	else
	{
		//document.getElementById("findet_head").innerHTML = "Consolidated";
		$("#findet_nav_1").removeClass('act');
		$("#findet_nav_2").addClass('act');		

		document.getElementById("findet_1").style.display = "none";
		document.getElementById("findet_2").style.display = "block";

		document.getElementById("findet_11").style.display = "none";
		document.getElementById("findet_22").style.display = "block";
	}
}
</script>

                    	<h2 class="hdr">About Maruti Suzuki</h2>

                        <div class="pc_abtinfo">

						 <p>Maruti Suzuki is in the Auto - Cars & Jeeps sector. The current market capitalisation stands at Rs 210,143.50 crore.<br /><br />The company management includes R C Bhargava - Chairman, K Ayukawa - Managing Director & CEO, T Hasuike - Director, T Suzuki - Director, K Saito - Director, O Suzuki - Director, K Ayabe - Director, K Yamaguchi - Director - Production, R P Singh - Independent Director, P Shroff - Independent Director, D S Brar - Independent Director, R S Karnad - Independent Director. <br /><br />It is listed on the BSE with a BSE Code of 532500 and the NSE with an NSE Code of MARUTI.<br /><br />Its Registered office is at 1, Nelson Mandela Road, Vasant Kunj,, New Delhi,Delhi - 110070.<br /><br />Their Registrars are Karvy Computershare Private Ltd.</p>    

                        	

                        </div>

                        <a href="javascript:void(0)" class="pc_handle more"></a>

<script>

function validateActionM()

{

	var search_guess_txt = jQuery.trim(document.getElementById("m3_stock_message_main").value);	

	if(search_guess_txt=='')

	{

		alert('Please enter stock name');

	}

	else

	{

		document.m3guess_stkMain.f_message.value =$('#m3_stock_message_main').val();

		document.m3guess_stkMain.submit();

		$('#m3_stock_message_main').val('');

	}

}

function m3GuessStockMain(frmname){ 

 	var search_guess_txt = jQuery.trim(document.getElementById("m3_stock_message_main").value);	

 	var top_search_type = 'Stocks';

 	var url = 'https://mmb.moneycontrol.com/india/messageboard/fetched.php?query='+escape(search_guess_txt)+'&f_criteria='+top_search_type+'&jsoncallback=?';

	jQuery('#feed-rhs').html('');

	if(search_guess_txt.length >= 3 && top_search_type=='Stocks'){

		jQuery('#feed-rhs').html('');

 		jQuery.ajax({

		url: url,

		dataType: 'jsonp',

		data: search_guess_txt,

		cache: false,

		success: function(d){ 

		jQuery('#feed-rhs').html('');

		jQuery.each(d, function(key, val) {

		jQuery('#feed-rhs').css('display','block');jQuery('#mmb-list-rhs').show();

		jQuery('#feed-rhs').append('<li  name="'+val.name+'" >' + val.caption + '</li>');

			if(search_guess_txt.toLowerCase()==val.name.toLowerCase())

			{

				document.getElementById("m3_stock_message_main").value='';

				document.getElementById("m3_stock_message_main").value=val.name;

				jQuery('#mmb-list-rhs').css('display','none');

				

			}

		});

		}

		});

	}else{jQuery('#mmb-list-rhs').hide();}



}	

jQuery('#feed-rhs > li').live('click',function(){

var sname='';

sname=jQuery(this).attr('name');



document.getElementById("m3_stock_message_main").value=sname;



jQuery('#mmb-list-rhs').hide();

});

</script>

<script>
function getcookie_add(name)
{
	var m_cookies = (document.cookie).split(";");
	for(m_ctr=0; m_ctr < m_cookies.length; m_ctr++)
	{
		m_str = (m_cookies[m_ctr]).split("=");
		if(m_str[0] == " "+name || m_str[0] == name)
			return m_str[1];
	}
	return "";
}
</script>
<script>
// user tracking
var expDays_usr = 90;
var exp_usr = new Date(); 
exp_usr.setTime(exp_usr.getTime() + (expDays_usr*24*60*60*1000));
var usrsitvis = getcookie_add('mcusrtrk');
if(!usrsitvis)
	usrsitvis = 1;
document.cookie = 'mcusrtrk' + "=" + escape(eval(parseInt(usrsitvis)+1)) +"; expires=" + exp_usr.toGMTString() + "; path=/;domain=.moneycontrol.com;";


function getkeywords() {
  var x = document.referrer;
  var keywords = 0;
  if (x.search(/yahoo/) != -1) {
			keywords = gup("p"); 
  }
  else if (x.search(/digg/) != -1) {
			keywords = gup("s"); 
  }
  else {
			keywords = gup("q"); 
  }
  keywords = truncate(keywords.replace(/\+/g, " "));
  return keywords; 
}

function truncate(input) {
  var byteLength = 61;
  return decodeURIComponent(encodeURIComponent(input)
.substr(0,byteLength));
}
function gup(name) {
  name = name.replace(/[\[]/,"\\\[").replace(/[\]]/,"\\\]");
  var regexS = "[\\?&]"+name+"=([^&#]*)";
  var regex = new RegExp( regexS );
  var results = regex.exec( document.referrer );
  if( results == null )
     return "";
  else
     return results[1];
}

function check_srchmail()
{
	if(document.getElementById("srchemail").value=='' || document.getElementById("srchemail").value=='Enter email address') 
	{
		document.frmsrhmail.srchemail.focus();
		return false;
	}
	else
		return true;
}

if(usrsitvis<=1)
{
	var kyd_type = 0;
	var s_keyword = getkeywords();	
	var price_kyd = "Maruti Suzuki";
	if(price_kyd.length>0 && s_keyword.length>0)
	{
		s_keyword = price_kyd;
		kyd_type = 1;
	}
	
	if(s_keyword.length>0)
	{
		$('#srchclout').load($.post('/mccode/common/get_srchnews.php?kyd='+escape(s_keyword)+'&key_type='+kyd_type, '', function(data) 
		{			
			$('#srchclout').html(data);		
		}));
	}
}

	function thomson_stk_reports(sc_id,sc_did){
		var url = 'https://www.moneycontrol.com/mccode/common/thomson_stat_ajax.php';
		var post_data = { 'sc_id' : sc_id, 'sc_did' : sc_did,'platform' : 'web' }
		$.ajax({
	      type: 'POST',
	      url: url,
	      data: post_data,	      
	      async: true,	      
	      dataType: "json",
	      success: function(data,status) {
	      		if(data['status']=='eroor'){
	      			mcloginsignin("signin");
	      		}else{
	      				// console.log(data['non_verified_user']);
						if(typeof(data['non_verified_user']) != "undefined" && data['non_verified_user'] !== null ){
		      			 	$("#thomson_popup").html(data['non_verified_user']);
		      			 }else if(data['is_subscribed']==1 && data['is_asset_scheduled']==1 ){
			       		 	$("#thomson_popup").html(data['subscribe_and_sheduled']);
			       		 }else if(data['is_subscribed']==1 && data['is_asset_scheduled']!=1 ){
			       		 	$("#thomson_popup").html(data['subscribe']);
			       		 	$("#thomson_popup_thanks").html(data['subscribe_thanks']);
			       		 }else if(data['is_subscribed']!=1){
			       		 	$("#thomson_popup").html(data['non_subscribe']);
			       		 }else if(data['status']=='eroor'){
			       		 	mcloginsignin("signin");
			       		 }
	       		}
	      	 }
		});

	}

		if($("#email_verify").val()==0 || $("#mobile_verify").val()==0){

			return false;
		}

		var product_id = $(pro).attr('product_id');
		$("#selected_product_id").val(product_id);
		var redirect_url = window.location; 
		$("#redirect_url").val(redirect_url);
		$("#back_url").val(redirect_url);
		$("#thomson_sub").submit();
	}

	function changeDownloadReportText(){
		$(".first_report").hide();
		if($("#report_download_count").val()==2){
			$("#report_download_count").val(1);
			$("#free_report_text").hide();
			$(".second_report").show();			
		}else if($("#report_download_count").val()==1){
			$("#report_download_count").val(0);
			$("#free_report_text").hide();
			$(".second_report").hide();
			$(".third_report").show();			
		}else if($("#report_download_count").val()==0){
			var sample_report_url = $("#sample_report_url").val();
			$("#non_subscribe_download").attr("href",sample_report_url);
		}
	}

 }
